## APPELLATE_HARM_EVIDENCE_EXTRACTION_COMPREHENSIVE_20260209.md
**Path:** `discovery\APPELLATE_HARM_EVIDENCE_EXTRACTION_COMPREHENSIVE_20260209.md`
**Time:** 18:44:20 | **Finds:** 3

- **Immediate**
